## p-e-w/heretic

> [!info]
> ⭐ 9,926 · Python · 2026-02-27  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/p-e-w/heretic)  
> `#Directional Ablation` `#Censorship Removal` `#Model Decensoring` `#Auto Parameter Tuning` `#abliteration` `#llm` `#transformer` 
> Heretic is a fully automatic censorship removal tool for transformer-based language models, combining directional ablation with TPE-based parameter optimization via Optuna. It automatically finds optimal abliteration parameters while co-minimizing refusals and KL divergence, producing decensored models without any human intervention.
> <sub>Fully automatic censorship removal for language models</sub>

> ⭐ 22,589 · Rust · 2026-03-02  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/rustfs/rustfs) · [Website](https://rustfs.com/download/)  
> `#Object Storage` `#Rust` `#S3-Compatible` `#Distributed Storage` `#ai-native` `#ai-storage` `#amazon-s3` `#bigdata` `#cloud-native` `#filesystem` `#minio` `#multi-cloud` `#object-storage` `#objectstorage` `#rust` `#s3` 
> RustFS is a high-performance, distributed object storage system built in Rust with full S3 compatibility. It delivers 2.3x faster performance than MinIO for 4KB object payloads, supporting migration and coexistence with MinIO and Ceph. Features distributed architecture, fault tolerance, Apache 2.0 license, optimized for data lakes, AI and big data workloads.
> <sub>🚀2.3x faster than MinIO for 4KB object payloads. RustFS is an open-source, S3-compatible high-performance object storage system supporting migration and coexistence with other S3-compatible platforms such as MinIO and Ceph.</sub>

> Nature is a general-purpose systems programming language and compiler implemented in pure C, compiling directly to native machine code without LLVM. > A pure Java library implementing the EGM96 Earth Gravitational Model to compute offset between WGS84 ellipsoid altitude and mean sea level altitude. Solves the problem of GPS devices returning ellipsoid height instead of MSL altitude by looking up EGM96 geoid offset values for given coordinates with interpolation.

> C++ implementation of HAT-trie based on the 2007 Askitis & Sinha paper, providing htrie_map and htrie_set classes. Efficiently stores string sets/maps by compressing common prefixes via array hash. ## tyxsspa/AnyText

> [!info]
> ⭐ 4,840 · Python · 2025-03-07  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/tyxsspa/AnyText)  
> `#Diffusion Model` `#Visual Text Generation` `#Text Editing` `#Multilingual` 
> AnyText is a diffusion-based framework for multilingual visual text generation and editing, featuring an auxiliary latent module and text embedding module to achieve precise text synthesis in images. It leverages an OCR encoder for glyph feature extraction and trains with text-control diffusion loss and text perceptual loss. Recognized as ICLR 2024 Spotlight, the project releases the AnyWord-3M dataset with 3M samples.
> <sub>Official implementation code of the paper <AnyText: Multilingual Visual Text Generation And Editing></sub>

> Official Apache connector integrating RocketMQ with Apache Flink. Provides RocketMQSource for reading messages and RocketMQSink for writing processed data. > <sub>RocketMQ integration for Apache Flink. This module includes the RocketMQ source and sink that allows a flink job to either write messages into a topic or read from topics in a flink job.</sub>

## lllyasviel/ControlNet

> [!info]
> ⭐ 33,670 · Python · 2024-02-25  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/lllyasviel/ControlNet)  
> `#Diffusion Model Control` `#Zero Convolution` `#Image Generation` `#Conditional Control` 
> ControlNet is a neural network architecture for conditional control of text-to-image diffusion models. By duplicating pretrained weights into trainable and locked copies with zero convolutions, it enables condition control without destroying the original model. Supports multiple control modalities including edge detection, depth estimation, and pose estimation, with efficient training on small datasets or personal devices.
> <sub>Let us control diffusion models!</sub>

## yc9559/uperf

> [!info]
> ⭐ 3,389 · Shell · 2022-09-04  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/yc9559/uperf)  
> `#Userspace Performance Tuning` `#CPU Frequency Control` `#Android System Optimization` `#Big Core Binding` 
> Uperf is an Android userspace performance controller enabling dynamic CPU tuning via sysfs nodes. It recognizes scenarios like app launches, screen states, and UI thread migrations, binding UI threads to big cores for improved responsiveness. Monitors Surfaceflinger rendering for proactive performance boosting, compatible with Android 6.0-12 and arm64 devices, installable via Magisk module or standalone deployment.
> <sub>Userspace performance controller for android</sub>

## netchx/netch

> [!info]
> ⭐ 17,439 · C# · 2026-03-01  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/netchx/netch)  
> `#Proxy Client` `#Shadowsocks` `#Traffic Control` `#Windows Networking` `#fullcone` `#netch` `#netfiltersdk` `#shadowsocks` `#shadowsocksr` `#socks` `#tun2socks` `#vless` `#vmess` 
> Netch is a Windows proxy client built on .NET 6.0, supporting multiple protocols including Shadowsocks, ShadowsocksR, WireGuard, Trojan, VMess, and VLESS. It offers four modes: process traffic interception (Netfilter), network sharing (WinPcap/Npcap), virtual adapter (TunMode), and web proxy, with UDP NAT FullCone compatibility for internet access and acceleration.
> <sub>A simple proxy client</sub>

## sharkdp/dbg-macro

> [!info]
> ⭐ 3,230 · C++ · 2026-02-14  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/sharkdp/dbg-macro)  
> `#C++ Debug Macro` `#Single-header Library` `#Runtime Inspection` `#Pretty-print` `#cpp` `#debugging` `#macro` `#pretty-printing` 
> A C++ debug macro inspired by Rust's dbg! macro, provided as a single-header library. The dbg(...) macro outputs variable values, expressions, types, file names, line numbers, and function names. Features colorized output, pretty-printing for containers, pointers, strings, enums and std::optional. Can be used directly in expressions and is compatible with C++11/14/17. Issues a compiler warning when included to remind removal before release.
> <sub>A dbg(…) macro for C++</sub>

## elunez/eladmin

> [!info]
> ⭐ 21,936 · Java · 2025-07-03  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/elunez/eladmin) · [Website](https://eladmin.vip/demo)  
> `#Spring Boot` `#JPA` `#RBAC` `#Admin Dashboard` `#admin` `#eladmin` `#element-ui` `#jpa` `#jwt` `#redis` `#spring-boot` `#spring-security` `#swagger2` `#vue` 
> A full-stack admin dashboard built with Spring Boot 2.7.18, JPA, and Vue3, featuring RBAC permission control, dynamic routing, and data dictionary management. Includes a code generator for rapid development, integrated with Redis caching, Quartz scheduling, service monitoring, and one-click deployment capabilities.
> <sub>eladmin jpa 版本：项目基于 Spring Boot 2.7.18、 Jpa、 Spring Security、Redis、Vue的前后端分离的后台管理系统，项目采用分模块开发方式， 权限控制采用 RBAC，支持数据字典与数据权限管理，支持一键生成前后端代码，支持动态路由</sub>
